focus_tree = {
	id = japan_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 30
			original_tag = JAP
		}
	}
	default = no
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 50 y = 2800 }


	#------------------------------------------------
	#INTERNAL DEVELOPMENT
	#------------------------------------------------
	#Saitama Shintoshin
	focus = {
		id = JAP_saitama_new_downtown
		icon = goal_JAP_const_saitama2
		x = 4
		y = 0
		cost = 10
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: focus JAP_saitama_new_downtown executed"
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -12 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			615 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = offices
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			add_victory_points = {
				province = 1097
				value = 2
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}

			}

				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_REFUSED_PROGRESSIVES
					}
					set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
				change_labour_unions_opinion = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_union_interest_TT
			}
			else_if = { #If they backtracked, don't give them anything!
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
					has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_REFUSED_PROGRESSIVES
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_union_interest_TT
			}

		}

	}
